北滿洪水爲災

Floods in Northern Manchuria Cause Disaster.

中東路派車救濟災民

The Chinese Eastern Railway Sends Vehicles to Aid Flood Victims.

（哈爾濱）七月十五日以來、連日大雨之結果、北滿一帶發生二十年來未有之大洪水、以哈爾濱爲中心、中東路東西南部各線、全部不通、目下哈爾濱完全陷於孤立之境、西部線方面、河川全部汜濫、住民陸續沿鐵道避難、向滿溝方面避難者、已有數千名、中東路本社、已由哈爾濱派大規模的急援列車、從事救恤、惟被洪水溺死者、已有數百、鐵道沿線難民冒雨前進、綿延不絕、如長蛇之陣、露宿雨中、無衣無食、慘不可言、而囤積各地之穀物、均被水冲去、數在廿餘萬石以上、（三日電通社電）

(Harbin) As a result of continuous heavy rains since July 15, a major flood unseen in twenty years has occurred in northern Manchuria. With Harbin as the center, all the east, west, south, and north lines of the Chinese Eastern Railway are blocked. Harbin is currently completely isolated. On the western line, all the rivers have overflowed, and residents are continuously taking refuge along the railway. Several thousand people have already taken refuge in the direction of Mangou. The headquarters of the Chinese Eastern Railway has sent large-scale emergency relief trains from Harbin to provide relief. However, hundreds of people have been drowned by the flood. Refugees along the railway are advancing in the rain, endlessly, like a long snake, sleeping in the rain without clothing or food, which is unspeakable. The grain stockpiled in various places has been washed away by the water, amounting to more than 200,000 shi. (3rd Dentsu News Agency Dispatch)

中央政治會議

Central Political Conference.

張羣任平文化整委會副會長

Zhang Qun appointed Vice Chairman of the Beiping Cultural Reorganization Committee.

黃郭繼任故宮博物院理事長

Huang Fu Succeeds as Chairman of the Board of Directors of the Palace Museum.

鐵顧呈請辭職由中政會慰勉

Gu Mengyu Requested Resignation, Praised by the Central Political Conference.

（南京）中央政治會議三日晨開會、汪兆銘主席、决議各案如下、（一）北平政務委員會委員增加十人、常務委員名額原定九人、茲改爲十一人、加推張羣·顧維鈞·王樹常·劉翼飛·易培基·石友三·孫殿英·劉尙清·王克敏·秦德純·爲北平政務委員會委員、並加派張羣劉哲爲常務委員、（二）指導整理北平市文化委員會副會長李煜瀛因赴法請求辭職、照准、聘任張羣爲指導整理北平市文化委員會委員、並指定爲該會副會長、（三）故宮博物院理事長李煜瀛辭職照准、以黃郛繼任、黃郛未到以前、由張羣代理、（四）確定民運航空主管權限案、交軍事經濟兩組審查、（五）委員兼南京市市長石瑛報告實際籌備地方自治發現種種困難、請設法救濟案、决議、南京市坊民大會可延緩舉行、關於選舉之法定人數、應依據内政部所定條文辦理、交行政院訓令南京市政府遵照、關於自治法規及推進自治問題交政治報告組法制組審查、（六）委員兼鐵道部長顧孟餘報告錄用職員馮建統經過情形、並稱因鐵道行政辦理困難、請准辭去鐵道部部長案、决議、由本會議慰勉、顧同志所請辭職之處、應毋庸議、至各報紙對錄用馮建統事有作誣蔑記載者、由本會議秘書處函請宣傳委員會加以嚴重警告、令其更正、（三日中央社電）

(Nanjing) The Central Political Conference was held on the morning of the 3rd, chaired by Wang Zhaoming. The following resolutions were made: (1) The number of members of the Beiping Political Affairs Committee was increased by ten. The original number of standing committee members was set at nine, but it has now been changed to eleven. Zhang Qun, Gu Weijun, Wang Shuchang, Liu Yifei, Yi Peiji, Shi Yousan, Sun Dianying, Liu Shangqing, Wang Kemin, and Qin Dechun were added as members of the Beiping Political Affairs Committee, and Zhang Qun and Liu Zhe were added as standing committee members. (2) Li Yuying, vice chairman of the Beiping Cultural Reorganization Committee, requested resignation due to going to France, which was approved. Zhang Qun was appointed as a member of the Beiping Cultural Reorganization Committee and designated as the vice chairman of the committee. (3) Li Yuying's resignation as chairman of the board of directors of the Palace Museum was approved, and Huang Fu was appointed as the successor. Before Huang Fu arrives, Zhang Qun will serve as acting chairman. (4) The case of determining the authority of the Civil Aviation Administration was handed over to the Military and Economic Groups for review. (5) Committee member and Nanjing Mayor Shi Ying reported on the various difficulties encountered in the actual preparation of local autonomy and requested assistance. It was resolved that the Nanjing Fangmin Congress could be postponed, and the legal number of electors for elections should be handled in accordance with the provisions set by the Ministry of the Interior. The Executive Yuan will issue instructions to the Nanjing Municipal Government to comply. The issue of autonomy laws and the promotion of autonomy was handed over to the Political Reporting Group and the Legislative Group for review. (6) Committee member and Minister of Railways Gu Mengyu reported on the circumstances of the recruitment of staff member Feng Jiantong and stated that due to the difficulty of handling railway administration, he requested approval to resign from the post of Minister of Railways. It was resolved that the conference would commend him. Gu's request to resign should not be discussed. As for the newspapers that have made slanderous records of the recruitment of Feng Jiantong, the Secretariat of this Conference will send a letter to the Propaganda Committee to give a serious warning and order them to correct it. (3rd Central News Agency Dispatch)

封鎖東北電政在當局考慮中

The Authorities Are Considering Blocking Telecommunications in the Northeast.

日方反向國際提說帖

The Japanese Side Submits a Memorandum to the International Community.

（南京）日人恐我國封鎖東北電政、曾向國際電政公會提出說帖、稱東北與國際之電信、日本有權代爲轉達、冀混亂世界聽聞、我國亦已向該會提出嚴重否認、在中國領土内之東三省、絕難容他國違法侵佔、關於封鎖辦法、當局正在審愼考慮中、將來實行後、全國電局、均停止接收發往日軍所佔據地點之各種電訊、同時拒接關外來電、並對於被佔區域内日軍及僞組織與各國來往電訊、亦一律拒絕轉遞、（三日專電）

(Nanjing) The Japanese, fearing that our country would block telecommunications in the Northeast, submitted a memorandum to the International Telecommunications Union, claiming that Japan had the right to relay telecommunications between the Northeast and the international community, hoping to confuse the world. Our country has also made a serious denial to the association. It is absolutely impossible to allow other countries to illegally occupy the three northeastern provinces within Chinese territory. Regarding the blocking methods, the authorities are carefully considering them. After implementation in the future, all telecommunications bureaus across the country will stop receiving all kinds of telegrams sent to the locations occupied by the Japanese army. At the same time, they will refuse to receive telegrams from outside the Shanhaiguan Pass. They will also refuse to forward all telegrams exchanged between the Japanese army and puppet organizations in the occupied areas and various countries. (3rd Dispatch)

日僑設郵便所外部將提抗議

The Ministry of Foreign Affairs Will Protest Against the Establishment of Post Offices by Japanese Residents.

(Nanjing) After investigation by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs and the Ministry of Communications regarding the unauthorized establishment of post offices by Japanese residents in various places, it was found that the post offices established by Japanese residents in Qingdao and Tianjin received mail sent to the Northeast without Chinese stamps, which seriously damages our country's sovereignty and destroys the Universal Postal Convention. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs has now compiled evidence and protested to Japan. If necessary, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs will issue a serious declaration to urge all countries in the world to pay attention and impose sanctions in accordance with international conventions. (3rd Dispatch)

京市成立血魂鋤奸團

The Blood Soul Anti-Treason Corps is Established in Nanjing.

（南京）京市血魂鋤奸團一日宣布成立、並發宣言、謂有團員數百、分佈全市、團員職業則農工商學黨政軍警各界均有、任務在調查事實、鋤減奸商、决不發生其他任何關係、如販買仇貨、經調查確實、警告無效者、即以炸彈手槍作最後解决、（三日專電）

(Nanjing) The Blood Soul Anti-Treason Corps of Nanjing announced its establishment on the 1st and issued a declaration stating that there are hundreds of members, distributed throughout the city. The members' occupations include agriculture, industry, commerce, academia, party, government, military, and police. The task is to investigate facts and eliminate treacherous merchants, and no other relationships will be formed. If enemy goods are sold, and the investigation is true and the warning is invalid, bombs and pistols will be used as the final solution. (3rd Dispatch)

Commercial News, Finance, Bullion, and Peaceful State: Only Three or Two Taels of Odd-Lot Trading; Yesterday's bullion market was very stable, with a firm trend and few fluctuations. In the morning and noon, there were only odd-lot trades of three or two taels. In the end, it rebounded by about three taels. However, the silver market continued to rise, and the exchange rate, although rising continuously, had no impact at all. The opening was slightly lower, and later there were slight ups and downs, revolving around 7434 taels. The buying interest from all parties was constant. As for foreign exchange bills, internal and external markets seemed to be diverging. The bank's cashiers were active and responsive, so people's confidence was good, and the market price was able to hold steady. Ultimately, it stood at around 745 taels. Because the next market will be Wednesday, there is usually no foreign exchange market, and the weather is still very hot, so it will remain closed for half a day. The details of what happened this morning are recorded below.

A Good Start of Two Taels and Eight Mace: From the early September futures opening, it fell slightly by two mace to 741 taels and eight mace. The big bars rose by another 1/16, and the American banks added 1/8. The forwards also continued to report large. However, the Guangdong banks Hengxing, etc., had already started buying. Then Dadecheng, Tong Taichang, Hengxing, and Yuan followed suit, and it increased from 1.6 mace to 3.2 mace. (However, it was heard that the gross trading initially made 40 taels with some change and then rose to 42 taels.) However, Yuanheng, Fuchang, etc., sold, and it retreated to two mace. Suddenly, it rose again. Hengxing, Fuxing, Yongyifeng, Yongheng, Yuanyuanmao, Yongyuankangxiang, etc., all deposited. For US dollars, the early settlement of October was 1.875, and September was 0.0625. Later, Maijia Li absorbed November at 0.375, and August was only calculated at 0.875. Then the price returned to the previous one tael and several mace. At 9:15, it was 3.7 mace. At that time, it was suppressed by a little over one mace, to two and a half mace. At 9:30, the British gold announcement remained unchanged, and the US dollar increased by 0.125, so the exchange rate was under pressure, but the gold market was still stable and instead increased to 3.5 mace. Internally, it seemed loose. The Shanghai September US dollar came out at 0.0625, and it retreated to 2.6 mace. Soon, because September only settled at 30 yuan, and Huabi absorbed November at 0.375, and Maihang absorbed 0.3125, and Hengxing also entered, and Fuchang, Hengyu, Fuyuanyuanxing, Yongzhifeng, Yongzhaofengchang, etc., buying intentions were agitated, and then raised 2 mace to nearly 44 taels and eight mace. After entering, there were slight turns of several mace. Then Dadecheng, Hengchang, Yongfuchang, Yuanheng, Daxing, Yongyifeng, Yongzhaofengchang, Tong Taichang, Yuhe, Futaiheng, etc., took advantage of this favorable price to sell one after another. Then the October US dollar could be settled at 0.125, and the bank bought November at 0.375. Maijia Li also bought forward British gold at 1.86875. For this reason, the gold price could not hold for long, and it fell by more than one tael. Around 10:30, it was 43 taels and four mace. In an instant, it increased by two or three mace. Unexpectedly, the selling wind did not stop. Hengyu, Yuanheng, Hongkangyong, Hengchangyong, etc., sold again and again. Furthermore, the November US dollar could be settled at 0.3125 and sold to the bank at 0.375, causing the market price to continue to fall by a little over two mace, to 41 taels and seven mace at 11:00. Soon after, Hengxing, Hengyuanyuan, Taizhifengyong, and goods hedging, etc., started competing to buy again. It is said that the current month's British gold Zhongfu Shanghai mutual trading was at 0.375 to 0.4375. Huabi absorbed the November US dollar at 0.3125, and September was still settled at 30 yuan. The market was sharp, and the price rebounded by three taels to 45 taels at 11:45. There were only turns of four or five mace in between. Then, because HSBC and others came out with October 30 yuan and 0.0125, and September 30 yuan, and some scattered bulls also vomited a little, it retreated to 4.23 mace and then rose to five mace. By the time of the noon closing at 44 taels and eight mace, the goods that came out were again traded at 4.12 mace. Finally, it was 3.4 mace, which Tong Taichang bought. Compared to the day before yesterday (according to the listed price), it rebounded by 2.8 mace. The maximum during the half-day was five mace, and the minimum was 1.6 mace. There were four differences of three taels. The bare bars increased by 8.5 mace. There were some transactions.

The Opening Price Is Suppressed by About 70 Taels: The opening price has been changed to 814 taels. Because the US dollar is listed higher by 0.125, it is estimated to be pressing around 70 taels. It is pressing five or six taels less than last month. The registered accounts for August and September are both 45 taels, and the makeup water is 43 taels.

Active Over-the-Counter Transactions: Over-the-counter transactions are still considered active, with more buyers. Stable Foreign Exchange Market: Yesterday, the silver market continued to report gains, and the exchange rate has also risen again. As for the impact on the local exchange market, HSBC's listed price was only a US dollar higher by 0.125, calculated at 29 yuan and a half. The German exchange rate increased by 0.025, and the Hong Kong exchange rate decreased by another 5 mace, to 76 taels and 0.875. The others, such as British, French, Dutch, Indian, and Singapore, all remained unchanged. It is said that the internal market was slightly turbulent after being stable in the morning, but it was stable at noon. However, the gold market reversed the potential upward trend. This is because people's confidence is strong and there are many seekers. By the time of the noon closing, compared to the previous evening, British and American gold had each shrunk by 0.0625, which is actually a clear stability and hidden firmness. The transactions on that day were quite active. There were some swap transactions by Fuchang and others, which were not few. The Market Situation Is Calm and Constant: Yesterday's market atmosphere was still energetic in the morning, but the afternoon market suddenly became weak. There was no sudden and drastic change. It is said that the silver and money industries, facing this chaotic period, had no interest in transactions, so they were unwilling to take any action. If there was an opportunity to take advantage of, they would not let others have it. This situation is really an unfortunate time for merchants.

Deposit Interest Set at Three Taels: The silver interest base for last month's deposit interest was less than three taels, as detailed in the previous day's newspaper. Yesterday, the industry association's standing committee decided that the deposit interest rate would be 3.95 taels, and the overdue interest would still be calculated at a fixed rate of 4.5 mace, and then added incrementally. In this way, the highest overdue interest would still not exceed 10 taels and 5 mace, which is similar to the situation in the past few months.

Cotton Yarn Market Returns After Falling: The cotton yarn market initially fell and then returned, and the trend was still stable. Most people's mentality was that actual sales were stagnant, and the US cotton inventory was too thick, tending to empty out. However, the current yarn stock of each factory has been greatly reduced compared to before, so the thinking of each factory is very good, and the financing is very relaxed. When it fell, some of them bought in to go long. Therefore, both long and short sides have considerable power. Now, the Sichuan gang is actively purchasing, but the amount of orders is not very enthusiastic. In short, the military unrest in the Northeast and the clouds of war are spreading, and people's hearts are greatly affected.

People's Cotton Market Atmosphere Is Mediocre: The opening of the People's Cotton Market was weak due to the fall in US cotton. The morale of the previous day was weak, and each month fell by one or two yuan. The market slowly rebounded in two or three rounds, and as a result, each month fell by two, three or five mace. The total transaction volume for the day was 31,600 bales. It was found that Changfeng sold 2,950 bales, Xiesheng 650 bales, Shenji 500 bales, and Tianlong 500 bales. Local News: The Guohua Coal Ball Company Robbed Twice in One Day

The first time at 7:00 AM

The second time to rob at noon

The police are deeply shocked

Total losses may reach three thousand gold

The Guohua Coal Ball Company at 394 Father Jin Road in the French Concession, has been established for many years and its business is quite developed. Unexpectedly, it has attracted the attention of bandits. What is most shocking is that it was robbed twice yesterday morning, setting a new record in Shanghai's robbery cases. The first incident occurred at 7:30 AM when the company had just opened its doors. Four robbers suddenly appeared, brandishing pistols, prohibiting any noise, and searching for about half an hour before escaping with the stolen goods. In this incident, the losses, including those of the tenant Yang Zhenhan's family, exceeded 2,500 yuan. Afterwards, the victim submitted a list of lost items to the police, requesting an investigation. The detective immediately dispatched patrolmen to investigate. When the patrolmen finished their investigation and returned to the police station to report, it was nearly 11:00 AM. Unexpectedly, less than twenty minutes after the patrolmen left the company, five more robbers arrived, most of whom spoke with a Shandong accent, each holding a pistol, forcing silence and carrying out a second robbery. They searched thoroughly, taking away about 200 yuan in cash and belongings before fleeing with the loot. The victim then continued to report to the police for the second time. The police expressed great shock upon inquiry and immediately ordered the patrolmen to pay close attention to ensure the case was solved.

Iron Factory Owner Blackmailed for 20,000 Gold

Payment Scheduled at North Zhejiang Road

A Woman Arrested While Collecting the Money

Chen Zhisheng, the owner of the De Taixiang Iron Factory located inside Qingfuli at the intersection of Fair Road and Zhoujiazui Road, received three blackmail letters on separate occasions the day before yesterday, demanding 20,000 yuan. Chen immediately reported this to the Huishan Police Station. However, due to inconsistencies in the location, the case was not solved. Yesterday, Chen received another blackmail letter from the "Seventh Group of the Third Route of the Chinese Communist Party," demanding 20,000 yuan and setting a deadline of 7:00 PM that day for the payment to be made in front of the Laoshunxintang Opium Cessation Public Office at 3 Hua'anfang, North Zhejiang Road. Chen immediately reported this to the Huishan Police Station at 3:00 PM that afternoon. However, because the meeting point was in the Chinese territory, the police station dispatched patrolmen to the No. 1 Branch of the Fourth District Public Security Bureau to inform them. The branch then sent two patrol officers and one detective to lie in ambush nearby. At around 7:15 PM, when Chen Zhisheng, the victim, arrived at the agreed location, he saw a woman around thirty years old standing in front of the public office. Chen approached her, and the woman asked if he was there to deliver the money. Chen replied yes, but he had only managed to gather 8,000 yuan. The woman took the money and gave Chen a receipt. At that moment, the ambushing police officers rushed forward and arrested her. At the same time, Qiu Xianrong, an employee of the opium cessation public office, was identified as a key suspect and was also arrested. They were temporarily detained in the No. 1 Branch of the Fourth District. The woman confessed that she was Ye Wushi, thirty years old, and lived at 31 Lai'anli, Baoshan Road. Afterwards, the Huishan Police Station, on the grounds that the victim resided in the concession, requested the No. 1 Branch of the Fourth District to hand over the male and female suspects for interrogation by the police station.

Apprentice Starts Fire in the Middle of the Night

Apprentice Claims to Be Dreaming

The Bizarre Case Deserves Thorough Investigation

Xu Yonglin, an eighteen-year-old apprentice from Haimen at the Rixin Laundry Company located at 2136 Peng Road, suddenly got up from his bedroom on the front floor at 3:15 AM the day before yesterday. He sneaked to the second floor and stole the iron door key from the waist of his fellow apprentice, Zhu Degen. He went downstairs, opened the iron door, took a cup of gasoline used for cleaning clothes, and found a box of matches in the kitchen. He then went back upstairs and threw the key back near Zhu Degen, who was sound asleep and completely unaware. Xu then went downstairs again, groped his way into the shop, took a stool, and went directly to the counter. He splashed the gasoline onto the piled-up paper boxes containing customers' clothes waiting to be washed in the closet. He then took out a match from his pocket and set the paper boxes on fire. Afterwards, he tried to climb down from the counter via the stool, intending to sneak back to his room. However, in his panic, he missed a step and fell to the ground. Shen Genan, another apprentice sleeping in the shop, was awakened by the noise and got up to investigate. Seeing the fire in the closet, he shouted for help. Xu pleaded with him not to call for help, but Shen continued to shout loudly. Chen Gaofeng, the owner of the laundry shop, who was sleeping upstairs, woke up from his dream and rushed downstairs. He entered the shop and saw more than a dozen paper boxes in the closet on fire. He used a cotton quilt to extinguish the fire, preventing a major disaster. When Xu Yonglin was questioned about the unprovoked arson, he stammered and refused to tell the truth. Therefore, Chen reported the incident to the Hongkou Police Station, which dispatched Chinese detective Liu Decheng to arrest Xu and take him to the police station for detention. He was then sent to the Fourth Criminal Division of the First Special District Court. According to police lawyer Zhang Tianyin, the circumstances of the case were bizarre. The defendant claimed at the police station that he was dreaming and completely unaware of the arson. The apprentice had been working at the Rixin Laundry Company for three months, and the owner, Chen Gaofeng, had not mistreated him. Furthermore, his past conduct was not bad. It was claimed that an unknown person, wearing a blue cloth short shirt and pants, threw a piece of paper at his head, causing him to become disoriented. As a result, Xu suddenly staged this terrible act that night. Chen Gaofeng, the owner of the company, and the apprentices Shen Genan and Zhu Degen, continued to testify about the situation. Chen also stated that the current losses included three pieces of customers' clothing that were burned, which would require compensation of about 100 yuan. He added that the defendant was usually clear-headed, had a good character, and was treated very well by him. When questioned about the confession, the defendant stated that he had gone out to buy noodles before the incident and met an unknown man on the road, about twenty years old, with a Shanghai accent, wearing a blue cloth shirt and pants. The man said he would introduce him to work elsewhere and slapped him on the head with a piece of colored paper before leaving. He returned to the shop and had nightmares that night, and all his actions were in a dream. He pleaded for understanding. Police lawyer Zhang also stated that he had learned that several apprentices had left the company before, and the defendant had previously worked as a laborer at a workshop. It was possible that he had been instigated by someone. The judge questioned him repeatedly and thoroughly, but the defendant insisted that the boss treated him well and that he was indeed acting in a dream. Judge Shen Bingrong ordered him to be remanded in custody and scheduled a date for sentencing.

Defense Statement of Xu Chongwen in Russian Beggar Case

Enumerates Facts and Legal Grounds

Regarding the death of the Russian named George Ratkeff, who died while begging, the warden Xu Chongwen has hired lawyer Zhao Chen to draft a defense statement, clarifying the facts and legal principles. The original statement is recorded below:

Defendant Xu Chongwen, right, selects and appoints defense lawyer Zhao Chen. Accuser Simon Grantke, Public Prosecutor: French Concession Police Department. For being prosecuted by the French Concession Police Department, in the case of the death of Russian prisoner George Ratkeff due to suspected abandonment, the facts are defended according to law. The prosecution in this case is purely based on collecting hearsay, catching shadows, and has no reliable evidence to convict people. The points that should be clarified in terms of facts and law are listed separately on the left.

(I) Clarification of Facts: (1) On the afternoon of June 17 this year, Xu Shunchen, the chief officer on duty at the detention center, issued a report stating that the newly admitted Russian prisoner George Ratkeff was admitted with an illness. The defendant immediately wrote on the original report form, "Immediately notify the doctor for proper treatment." This form has now been submitted as evidence, which proves that the defendant immediately instructed the doctor to diagnose and treat the sick Russian prisoner when he was admitted. There was absolutely no abandonment, one. (2) At 5:00 PM on June 17, Dr. Yu Honggao followed orders to come to the detention center for an examination and treatment. He used relief water to treat him and clear summer heat. The next day, his condition was still peaceful, and he was given Lilihua Ping'an Powder, one dose each in the morning and afternoon, and his condition was gradually alleviated. This has been submitted as evidence in the form of Dr. Yu's diagnosis report, which can be used as proof. It shows that the deceased Russian prisoner continued to receive diagnosis and treatment after he was admitted to the detention center, and there was no abandonment, two. (3) At about 10:00 AM on the 19th, the guard suddenly came to report that the deceased Russian prisoner had suddenly changed his condition. Because the doctor did not live in the detention center, the defendant immediately ordered the guard Dai Shouhua to run to No. 18 Jijiwu Lane, West Gate, to invite Dr. Yu to come for treatment as soon as possible. The doctor arrived at the detention center at 11:00 and immediately gave him treatment. He diagnosed that his condition was very serious and that he needed to be sent to the hospital for treatment. Unfortunately, that day was a Sunday holiday, so the court and prosecutor's office were closed, making it impossible to report. It was planned to send him to the hospital first, but it was raining heavily that day, and the detention center had no telephone and no ambulance. It was not appropriate to hire a rickshaw or send him on a stretcher to the hospital. It was also planned to borrow the court's official car for escort, but it was not available because it was a holiday. At this time, it was around 11:30. The deceased Russian prisoner was sweating profusely and on the verge of death and almost impossible to save. It was planned to order the guard to go to Father Jin Road area to hire a car to send him to the hospital, but it was too late. This is the actual situation. There are many doctors and staff members in the detention center, and they cannot hide it. The defendant has done his duty and cannot save him, but he is truly free of guilt. This is based on the fact that the defendant absolutely did not abandon the deceased Russian prisoner before his death, three. (4) The French Concession Police Department filed the prosecution purely based on the one-sided accusation of the Russian Simon Grantke, who claimed to be the deceased's brother. And Simon Grantke is based on the slander of witnesses Gu Lutuo Jin, Kevos Yigufu and Shan Putuo Laifu. On the one hand, he said that your brother was beaten to death by the staff of the detention center, and on the other hand, he said that your brother was sick and the detention center did not give him medical treatment, so he died. Not to mention whether he died from injury or illness, the circumstances are very different. If he died from illness, he should not say that he died from injury. If he died from injury, he should not say that he died from illness. His words are contradictory and not worth adopting. Even just based on the testimonies of the witnesses in the French Concession Police Department's investigation of the case on July 4 and the testimonies made by the court during the trial on July 11, they all said that the deceased was not beaten in the detention center, and they unanimously denied that the brother of the deceased had reported that he was injured to death. If you can draw inferences from one instance, the testimonies of the witnesses on the part of the death from injury are inconsistent and very different before and after. Therefore, the testimonies on the part of the abandonment to death are also sufficient to prove that they are nonsense and have ulterior motives, and are not worth adopting at all. Although the witnesses stated that the deceased was not given medical treatment in the detention center, a review of the testimony of the witness Kevos Yigufu during the trial on July 11 shows that the official asked the witness Kevos Yigufu, "After entering the detention center, did the doctor treat him?" He replied, "No medical treatment was given." He was also asked, "Was he given any medicine to eat?" He replied, "I only saw him drink water twice, and I didn't see any medicine," etc. The words "drank water twice" refer to the medicine given by the doctor. The light in the detention center was insufficient, and the witness and others were detained in the same detention center and could not see clearly. Furthermore, the witness could not understand the language when the medicine was delivered to the detention center. Moreover, what method did this Kevos Yigufu use to determine whether it was water or medicine? Since he did not personally taste the medicine, he could not arbitrarily say it was water. The doctor only has the obligation to treat the patient, and has no obligation to report to the fellow prisoners that he is treating the patient. The witness is making slanderous remarks, how can he be believed? This is based on repeated consideration of the testimonies of the witnesses. The contradictory words are self-defeating, and are sufficient to prove that the defendant did not abandon the deceased Russian prisoner, four. (5) As the warden of the detention center, the defendant is responsible for directing and supervising all the staff and managing all the affairs of the detention center. All the dozens of books and registers that should be prepared in the detention center are tasks that must be personally reviewed every day, as well as all other internal and external affairs, which are extremely busy. It is impossible for a sick Russian prisoner to devote all his energy to one person and ignore all the affairs of the detention center. Moreover, before the deceased Russian prisoner died, he had already ordered the doctor to give him proper treatment. Moreover, Dr. Yu's testimony during the trial on July 11 also stated that "Of course, I must follow the warden's order before I can enter the detention center for treatment. Otherwise, I cannot directly enter the prison cell." The official also asked, "Did you finally get the warden's order?" Yu replied, "I did get the warden's order." This proves that the defendant has always been diligent in his duties. If it is said that the deceased Russian prisoner died in the detention center, then he should be held responsible for abandonment. Then there should never be any deaths from illness in prisons in all civilized countries, otherwise their prison officials will all become guilty of abandonment. Is there any reason in the world? Based on this reasoning, it is also sufficient to prove that the defendant did not abandon him, five.

(II) Legal Clarification: (1) According to the French Concession Police Department's indictment and transmittal form, the defendant is prosecuted for suspected abandonment resulting in death under Article 310, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Law. A review of the special constituent elements of the crime of abandonment resulting in death under Article 310, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Law shows that it is nothing more than: 1. The abandoned person is a person without the ability to save himself; 2. For a person without the ability to save himself, he has the responsibility to provide assistance, nurture and protection according to laws, regulations or contracts; 3. There is an act of abandonment, or failure to provide the assistance, nurture and protection necessary for his survival; 4. This results in death. If any of these elements are missing, it cannot be established. Moreover, there must be a direct causal relationship between the act of abandonment and the result of death, otherwise the crime cannot be established. The deceased Russian prisoner George Ratkeff was indeed a person without the ability to save himself, and the defendant did have a legal responsibility to protect him. But during the three days he was in the detention center, he ordered the doctor to give him diagnosis and treatment without interruption. According to the initial diagnosis, his illness was not very serious. According to the subsequent report, his illness was about to be alleviated, and there was no danger of transmission. If it is considered contagious, why did the three Russian prisoners in the same room not develop the disease, and most of the prisoners detained together did not contract the disease? In this case, there was no need to send him to the hospital for treatment immediately. Unexpectedly, at 11:00 AM on June 19, his illness suddenly became serious, and he died before he could be sent to the hospital. This was due to time constraints. How can it be determined that he was abandoned just because he was not sent to the hospital? The defendant provided the necessary protection and did not abandon him. As for his death, it was a natural and irresistible result of sudden illness and death. It cannot be proven that it has a causal relationship with the defendant's actions. Therefore, the prosecutor's contrived and far-fetched accusations are obvious without saying more. This is based on the legal clarification, one. (2) The establishment of a crime requires an active or passive act in terms of objectivity, and the act must be illegal, and the illegal act must result in the infringement of legal interests. However, in terms of subjectivity, there must also be criminal intent. The crime under Article 310, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Law naturally takes intentional abandonment as a prerequisite for whether a crime is established. In this case, the defendant did not have an active, passive, or illegal act of abandonment, and the death of the deceased Russian prisoner cannot be proven to have any direct causal relationship with the defendant. Then, based on objectivity, there is no room for the crime of abandonment resulting in death to be established. As for subjectivity, what hatred or hatred does the defendant have with the deceased Russian prisoner? Why is it necessary to put him to death? The funds in the detention center were originally around 30 yuan, but in recent months, they have often exceeded 100 yuan. This shows that the police department only relies on the one-sided lies of the witnesses, and does not have an active way to prove that the defendant has the subjective responsibility of malicious abandonment. Then, according to Article 24 of the Criminal Law, acts that are not intentional are not punished. It is impossible to constitute the crime of abandonment resulting in death. This is based on the legal clarification, two. (3) According to Article 50 of the Provisional Rules for Detention Centers promulgated and revised by the Ministry of Justice on May 3, 1919, "When a defendant is ill, he shall be treated by a doctor. If he is seriously ill, he shall be transferred to the hospital. In case of critical illness, his family members shall be notified and the court or prosecutor shall be reported." After the deceased entered the detention center, he repeatedly ordered the doctor to give him treatment. When his illness was critical, although he wanted to report to the court and transfer him to the hospital, it was too late to save him. This is not in violation of the provisions of that article. He has asked himself and feels that he has not failed in his duty. This is based on the rules of the detention center. The defendant did not neglect his duties and should not bear criminal responsibility for abandonment resulting in death, three. Based on the above conclusions, the court should carefully investigate and, based on the reason that the defendant's suspicion of committing a crime cannot be proven under Article 316 of the Criminal Procedure Law, announce a verdict of not guilty in order to clear the wrong and secure his job. This is for the public good. Sincerely submitted, Shanghai Second Special District Local Court Criminal Division. Defendant Xu Chongfu, selected and appointed defense lawyer Zhao Chen, wrote the statement on August 3, 1921.

Guo Luman's Marriage Dispute Resolved

Separated from the Female Painter

The Wife, Ms. Han, Returns to Good Terms

The Public Prosecution for Perjury Is Still in Question

The Female Painter Will Apply for Withdrawal

Since Guo Luman, a native of Ningbo, held a wedding ceremony with the female painter Xu Zhiqing, it has caused a great uproar, resulting in as many as six lawsuits in the First Special District Court: (1) Guo's wife, Ms. Han, requested the police to file a public prosecution against Guo for bigamy; (2) Guo's wife, Ms. Han, filed a private prosecution against Xu Zhiqing, Xu Guanchen, Lian Jiming, and Xing Chunhua for knowingly marrying and helping bigamy; (3) Guo filed a civil suit against Ms. Han, claiming that her identity was unclear and requesting confirmation; (4) Xu Zhiqing filed a private prosecution against Guo Luman, Guo's wife, Ms. Han, Han Meisheng, and Hu Miaosheng for fraudulent marriage; (5) The prosecutor filed a public prosecution against Han Meisheng and Hu Miaosheng for perjury; (6) Han Meisheng and Hu Miaosheng filed a private prosecution against Xu Zhiqing for forging private documents. Among the six cases, the two cases of confirming identity and fraudulent marriage have been ruled by the court to be suspended. The remaining cases have been accepted by Criminal Division Chief Feng Shide and are being investigated jointly. The details of the repeated court hearings will be reported in this newspaper. It is learned that Ms. Guo Han, Xu Zhiqing, and Guo Luman all feel that the situation is extremely bad. If they continue to litigate, they will definitely suffer both losses. Therefore, they urgently sought reconciliation. The other day, all parties gathered at the law firm of Guo Luman's legal advisor, Lawyer Dang Ganghou, to discuss reconciliation methods and conditions. After discussing until 2:30 AM, they finally found a proper solution and signed a contract. The terms were roughly that Guo Luman would separate from Xu Zhiqing, and Guo would pay Xu a large amount of compensation. Guo and Ms. Han would return to good terms, and the rental income from the properties that Guo should receive would be split equally. For all lawsuits, except for the public prosecution requesting the police and prosecutor not to pursue the matter, all private prosecution cases would be withdrawn from the court. Yesterday morning, Judge Feng and Prosecutor Wu Xiangzu and Clerk Tang Weishu continued the hearing of the case. Only three defendants, Guo Luman, Han Meisheng, and Hu Miaosheng, reported. Guo Han's attorney, Yang Linzhi, stated that the case had been fully reconciled through the mediation of the Guo and Han families, and the lawsuits would be withdrawn separately. However, this morning, lawyer Tan of Han Mei and Hu Miaosheng did not agree to withdraw the lawsuit against Xu Zhiqing for forging documents because he was not sure whether the prosecutor's public prosecution could be withdrawn. Therefore, Xu's attorney, Chen Tingrui, also did not agree to withdraw the fraudulent marriage lawsuit. My clients also cannot withdraw the lawsuit. If the prosecutor withdraws the perjury lawsuit, then the entire case can be concluded. Moreover, Lawyer Chen has already filed a statement (recorded separately) to the court, stating that he does not want to delve into the perjury matter. Therefore, the key to this case depends entirely on whether the prosecutor can withdraw the public prosecution. This should be stated to the court and requested a ruling. Police lawyer Ru Baoyi stated that the police's public prosecution cannot be withdrawn, so they would not interfere with their reconciliation. However, one point that should be noted by the court is whether the prosecutor's filing of a public prosecution against Han Meisheng and Hu Miaosheng in court is legal. A review of the second half of Article 5 of the New Agreement returned to the court stipulates that "all investigation procedures of the prosecutor are open, and the defendant's lawyer is allowed to make statements in court." Therefore, the prosecutor's indictment must first be investigated in court. However, Chief Prosecutor Wang did not go through the above procedures and declared a public prosecution in court. This is obviously contrary to the agreement. Therefore, his prosecution is illegal and the court should consider the situation and make a ruling. Lawyer Tan Yigong of Han and Hu stood up to oppose the prosecutor's public prosecution. Judge Feng reviewed the evidence and stated that the legality of the prosecutor's public prosecution in this case still needs to be studied, so he ordered the case to be adjourned to next Friday for another hearing before adjourning the court. The application of Xu Zhiqing to the court is recorded below for application matters. I, Zhiqing, was ordered to summon Han Meisheng and Hu Miaosheng to court as witnesses in the case of knowingly marrying Guo Han. Later, due to the occurrence of perjury, Zhiqing filed a complaint with the prosecutor of the court, and the prosecutor filed a public prosecution. I have learned that Zhiqing and Guo Han's case has been reconciled by both parties, and Zhiqing does not want to pursue the perjury part of Han Meisheng and Hu Miaosheng, nor does she want Han Meisheng and Hu Miaosheng to be punished. Therefore, in accordance with the provisions of Article 264 of the Criminal Procedure Law, I request to withdraw the public prosecution before the start of the trial.

Wu Jian'guang's Son Accused of Seduction, Continued Hearing

Wu's Son Files Counterclaim

The Statements of Both Parties Differ Greatly

Wu Zhongliang, a 27-year-old native of Meizhou, Guangdong, is the son of the famous astrologer Wu Jian'guang. He lives at 17 Shishanli, Yuanfang Road. Recently, Shen Aie, a 21-year-old female employee of the Apex Commercial Printing House on Jiujiang Road, from Wuxi, and her mother, Shen Chu, hired lawyer Xue Jiaqi to accuse Wu of seducing their daughter, etc. Judge Wu Tingqi has held two hearings, but the defendant Wu Zhongliang failed to appear and was ordered to be arrested. Wu heard that the court had issued an arrest warrant, knew that he could not escape, so he hired lawyer Zheng Wenkai to defend him, and submitted a defense statement, stating the details of the various circumstances, and filed a counterclaim against Shen Chu and her daughter. Yesterday afternoon, the case was scheduled for a continued hearing. The plaintiff, Shen Aie, wearing a red printed cheongsam, white canvas shoes, and flesh-colored stockings, arrived at the court with her mother around 2:00 PM and sat in the witness seat. However, her attorney, Xue, had not arrived in court by the time the case was heard. The defendant, Wu Zhongliang, also arrived at the court with lawyer Zheng and surrendered himself. Judge Wu first questioned Shen Chu, who stated that she was accusing the defendant of abducting her daughter, and recounted the details, saying how the defendant and her daughter met and developed a relationship, and that she did not know about it at the time because they kept it secret. It was not until January of this year that she saw Aie's stomach getting bigger and knew that something was wrong. Under her strict questioning, Aie told her the whole story, saying that she had been lured to the Central Hotel and Hong Kong Hotel by the defendant on September 22 and 28 of last year, and had been raped, resulting in a secret pregnancy. She is now demanding that the defendant be punished with appropriate punishment. Shen Aie stated that she was 21 years old, born on the eighth day of the twelfth month of the first year of the Republic of China, and her zodiac sign is the rat. She is in charge of making letter sets at the Apex Commercial Printing House on Jiujiang Road and must pass Nanjing Road every day. The defendant works at the Fengyu Foreign Firm on the Bund and must also pass Nanjing Road. In June of last year, she met the defendant on the road, and the defendant secretly followed her. Since then, he has followed her every day. On August 8, he struck up a conversation with her and followed her to her home at 209 Jiuanli, Aixierjin Road, and then invited her to go out with him. At that time, her female colleague Lu Xiumei was also there. The three of them went out together, first to the Daguanlou for dinner, and then to the Zhejiang Grand Theater to watch a movie, taking the opportunity to inquire about her family background. She replied that her family had her mother and three sisters. The defendant said that he was not yet married and wanted to marry her. On August 15, he invited her to the Pin Fang Photography Studio in the City God Temple to take a photo. Because it was not clear, they went to the Meihua Photography Studio on August 20 to take a photo of each of them, and also took a photo together. The two photos were taken away by the defendant, saying that he would show them to his mother and ask someone to act as a matchmaker. She then presented the photo taken with the defendant, saying that this photo was reprinted from the negative of the Meihua Photography Studio, and recounted the details of being lured to the Central and Hong Kong Hotels to open rooms together by the defendant. Her statement was seen in the previous lawsuit, which is omitted. The defendant, Wu Zhongliang, stated that what the Shen mother and daughter had said was not true. He explained that at 6:00 PM on September 17 of last year, he was watching a civilized play at the roof garden of the Wing On Company when he happened to see Shen, and their seats were next to each other. They asked and answered each other about the plot of the play, and he inquired about her name, address, and domicile, which he truthfully told her. At that time, he lived on Fusheng Road. Shen said that his father was Wu Jian'guang, a famous astrologer, and expressed great admiration, and said that she lived in Jiuanli, which was close to each other, and they could visit each other from time to time. Two days later, on Saturday, he went to the railway station to visit a friend and was on his way home when he passed Shen's door. He happened to meet Shen and was invited to sit down and chat. Then Shen introduced him to Shen Aie and asked about her age. She said she was 22 years old, her zodiac sign was the dog, and she was working in the printing house. Shen wanted to keep him for dinner at home. He said that socializing between men and women should be open, so he invited her mother and daughter to the Daguanlou for Western food and to watch a movie. In mid-autumn in August, Shen wanted to go to the City God Temple to burn incense and invited him to accompany her. He agreed and went with Shen's mother and daughter. Passing by the Weixin Photography Studio, Aie wanted to take a photo, so they went inside. Aie took a photo alone. Because it was not clear, a few days later, he went to Meihua with Aie and her sister Ainan to take another photo. Aie expressed her willingness to take a photo with him, so the two took a photo together. This is the actual situation. As for why she came to sue, it may be because Shen asked him to borrow 200 yuan, and although he did not refuse at the time, he immediately stopped going there and therefore held a grudge. At this point, Judge Wu ordered that the hearing be closed to the public, so about a hundred men and women who were listening to the hearing were turned away. The defendant continued, saying that the opening of the room, etc., mentioned by the plaintiff were all fabricated. Because every time he went to the plaintiff's house or went out with Aie, her mother or sister would always go with them, and there was never a private outing between the two of them. As for taking a photo together, it was true, but Shen Chu was also present at the time. He has a wife at home, who he has been married to for three years, and he cannot marry another wife and commit bigamy. In short, the plaintiff's side wants him to be subjected to criminal punishment and achieve their goal of defrauding him of money. Hearing this, Shen Chu said that what the defendant had said was not true. She had never visited the Wing On Company for recreation. Her daughter must go to Apex to work every day without interruption. She would come home after 5:00 PM and never spend the night out or not return home one night. Shen Aie also said that she was lured to the Central Hotel by the defendant at 3:00 PM on September 22, and opened room 220 at the Hong Kong Hotel at 4:00 PM on September 28. Lawyer Xue had gone to the Hong Kong Hotel to investigate this matter and confirmed that Wu Zhongqi, i.e., the defendant's pseudonym, had gone to open a room on that day. Lawyer Xue could not come to court today due to a cold. Judge Wu reviewed the evidence and stated that it was still necessary to reschedule the case, so he ordered the defendant to leave and the case to be rescheduled for another hearing in seven days.

Huining School Holds Ancient and Modern Calligraphy and Painting Exhibition

The Huining School on Glock Road in this city regularly holds an exhibition of ancient and modern calligraphy and paintings during the holidays. This year's collection of famous works, ancient and modern, is particularly rich. It has been decided to open the exhibition to the public at the school for six days, starting today (the 4th) and ending on the 10th of this month. All circles are welcome to visit. It is heard that recent works by famous artists such as Huang Binhong, which are not easily seen outside, will be exhibited, which is sure to be a grand occasion. It is also heard that Ms. Huang Yingfen, the niece of Mr. Huang Binhong, has formed a women's calligraphy and painting society with Ms. Gu Mufei and Ms. Zhu Guanying, and will soon have their works on display.

Fire at Dengtu Road Yesterday Morning

Five Houses Burned Down

Losses of 70,000

At 1:35 AM yesterday morning, a fire broke out in a raincoat store at 666 Dengtu Road near Broadway Road due to carelessness. At the same time, it spread to the woodworking shop at 665 and the canvas shops and confectionery stores at 667, 668, and 669. For a time, black smoke filled the air and the flames raged. Fortunately, the Hongkou Fire Brigade arrived after hearing the news and was able to extinguish the fire. The houses at 665 to 667 were completely destroyed. It is reported that the losses are estimated to be over 70,000 yuan. The other two houses also suffered heavy losses.

Reenactment of the Bolivia-Paraguay Drama　翰

Recent international news. Relations between Bolivia and Paraguay in South America have suddenly deteriorated again. Bolivia is bombing Paraguayan border fortresses with airplanes. Paraguay has also issued a mobilization order, preparing for war. Argentina, Brazil, Chile, and three other countries have come forward to mediate, but have been rejected. The actions between the two countries seem to be trending towards an extreme situation.

The animosity between Bolivia and Paraguay has a long history. Between the two countries, there is a territory called the Chaco, covering an area of 100,000 square miles. The land is fertile, leading to disputes over ownership that have persisted for years. It is a well-known border issue in South America. In December 1928, Bolivia and Paraguay had a major dispute. The degree of their discord was tantamount to an undeclared war. Both Bolivia and Paraguay were members of the League of Nations. At that time, the 53rd session of the League of Nations Council was being held in Locarno. Under the leadership of Briand, telegrams were sent to both countries to stop the war, urging them to fulfill their international obligations and abide by the League of Nations charter. However, both countries continued to argue, disregarding the League of Nations' advice. As a result, Briand's desire for a glorious resolution like the Bush dispute of 1925 was unattainable. The League of Nations' authority had already been largely lost at that time.

Moreover, at that time, the Jinan Incident occurred in the Far East. Its severity far exceeded the animosity between Bolivia and Paraguay. Our country appealed to the League of Nations, but the League of Nations ignored it, focusing solely on mediating the dispute between Bolivia and Paraguay, as if it genuinely wanted to fulfill its mission of international peace. In the end, it was merely a scene in the European and American power struggle. The United States, based on the Monroe Doctrine as its international policy, does not allow interference from countries outside the Americas in matters of the Americas. It uses the Pan-American Conference as a tool to control the small countries of the Americas, acting as the overlord of the Americas and opposing the League of Nations in Geneva. The European powers are scheming to break the Monroe Doctrine. Furthermore, the dispute between Bolivia and Paraguay occurred when the newly elected President Hoover was on a tour of South America. The League of Nations wanted to use this to mock the incompetence of the United States. Subsequently, Bolivia and Paraguay ultimately disregarded the warnings of the League of Nations and only accepted the mediation of the Pan-American Conference. Therefore, the Pan-American Conference passed a compulsory arbitration and compulsory reconciliation resolution. The Bolivia-Paraguay drama was temporarily concluded.

However, the Pan-American Conference's handling of the dispute between Bolivia and Paraguay did not fundamentally resolve the issue. It only sought temporary stability, leaving the ownership of the Chaco region unresolved, creating a source of continuous conflict between Bolivia and Paraguay. Therefore, the current incident is by no means without cause. It is merely a continuation of the drama in the winter of 1928. It is difficult for us to predict whether this drama will continue to expand. However, we can confidently assert that the United States will come forward as the leader of the Americas to mediate, thereby maintaining the facade of the Monroe Doctrine. As for the League of Nations, it has been ridiculed and attacked by Japan due to the Sino-Japanese incident, and is in a difficult situation. Even if it wants to send telegrams and sing high praises again as in the winter of 1928, how can it be possible?

What lessons does the Bolivia-Paraguay dispute provide us? The authority of the League of Nations is no longer capable of being revitalized. Today's international peace is merely a temporary stability between nations. What imperialism wants to maintain is merely a state of temporary stability between nations, and it has no genuine desire to cultivate the foundation of peace. The resolution of international disputes addresses the symptoms rather than the root causes, and there is never a thorough plan. The reenactment of the Bolivia-Paraguay drama is a gift of this kind of incomplete international peace. The stones from other hills can be used to polish jade. In light of the dispute between Bolivia and Paraguay, and in the state of international anarchy, is there any other way to survive other than striving for self-strengthening and resisting to the death? Now, Jehol is in critical condition, and North China is in a dangerous situation. If there are still people who want to continue to beg for international intervention as the only policy of resisting Japan, they are truly stubborn and unenlightened. Discussing the animosity between Bolivia and Paraguay, I cannot help but think of our serious national crisis, and I am filled with anxiety.

Domestic Important Telegrams

Valiant Army Fiercely Attacks Yingkou

Fierce fighting with Japanese troops from the night before last to last night had not yet stopped.

The Haicheng Concession is Surrounded, Many Japanese Residents Flee to Barracks

(Tokyo) Today, the fighting near Yingkou is still ongoing. "Bandits" are currently fighting against Japanese naval and army soldiers and the "Manchukuo" army. It is reported that there are many casualties on both sides. Fighting is also taking place in Haicheng, 15 miles northwest of Dashiqiao, and other locations. Japanese reinforcements are currently rushing to the war zone. Residents in the war zone are extremely panicked, and many women and children are fleeing to the barracks. Retired soldiers have now been called out to take on the duty of guarding the troops. According to Japanese news, the "bandits" are the volunteer army of Zhang Xueliang, who are disturbing the South Manchurian Railway area under Zhang's orders. (3rd Reuters dispatch)

(Beiping) The Japanese Embassy here received a telegram from Shenyang describing the situation of so-called "bandits" attacking the Niuzhuang Yingkou area. It said that about 1,000 irregular troops began attacking Niuzhuang yesterday morning (Tuesday). The defending troops, numbering only 250, still repelled the attacking army. Fighting occurred intermittently during the day. At night, the enemy army launched another general attack but were repelled. "Manchukuo" aircraft participated in the battle, twice dropping bombs on the enemy army near Niuzhuang yesterday. The last telegram received by the embassy was sent at 3:00 a.m. this morning. At that time, fighting was still ongoing in the area near Niuzhuang. The Japanese Embassy also stated that Haicheng was attacked yesterday, but the outcome is unknown. (3rd Reuters dispatch)

(Dalian) The Liaoxi Volunteer Army retreated to its original defenses at dawn this morning to discuss strategies for attacking Yingkou again. At 10:30 a.m., they proceeded towards Yingkou. After receiving a report from an airplane, the Japanese army ordered Japanese residents to evacuate first at 2:30 p.m. The third major battle of Yingkou is imminent. (3rd China United Press dispatch)

Volunteer Army Attacks Haicheng Three Times

(Dalian) Two hundred members of the Liaoxi Volunteer Army besieged Haicheng at 8:30 p.m. last night, engaging in battle with Japanese troops for more than an hour. They feigned defeat and retreated. The Japanese, unaware, went to bed at ease. At 10:30 p.m., more than a thousand volunteer soldiers attacked Haicheng again, surrounding the South Manchurian Railway concession from the east, west, and north. The Japanese army then realized that they had fallen into a trap and hastily fought back. Fearing for the safety of the Japanese residents, they ordered more than 400 Japanese residents to take refuge in the railway garrison barracks and urgently telegraphed the Japanese army headquarters in Shenyang for reinforcements. Upon hearing the news, the headquarters immediately ordered the Handa unit to rescue them. They departed from Shenyang by train at 11:00 p.m. However, at 12:30 a.m., the volunteer army sent a detachment to destroy the railway and telegraph and telephone lines. The train from Shenyang to Dalian last night stopped at Anshan upon hearing the news. As of this morning, telegraphs and telephones are still not working. This morning, the volunteer army attacked Haicheng for the third time. The Japanese army, unable to guarantee the lives and property of the Japanese residents, again ordered the Japanese residents to take refuge from the barracks to Dashiqiao or Dalian. The faces of the evacuating Japanese residents were pale, trembling with fear, and their condition was extremely miserable. (3rd China United Press dispatch)

High Alert Along the South Manchurian Railway

(Dalian) Since the night of August 1st, after the Liaoxi Volunteer Army actively attacked Changchun, Shenyang, Haicheng, and Yingkou along the South Manchurian Railway, the Japanese army headquarters has become tense. Japanese residents initially believed that the South Manchurian Railway concession was an absolutely safe zone. After being attacked in various places, they still believed that the Japanese army was strong enough to cope. However, after several panics, they began to doubt. Japanese residents, who usually regarded the lives of Chinese people as worthless and encouraged the Japanese army to kill them, are now pale and terrified, unable to sleep peacefully, and business has stopped. Last night, the Japanese army headquarters and the South Manchurian Railway authorities ordered Japanese residents in various places to arm themselves and be on guard, including stationmasters and below, who were armed and on guard all night. The headquarters also convened various staff officers to study countermeasures. If the security of the South Manchurian Railway cannot be maintained, the Japanese economic institutions in the Northeast will inevitably go bankrupt. The war along the South Manchurian Railway has dealt a huge blow to Japan, far exceeding the wars in various parts of North Manchuria. Its significance can be known. (2nd China United Press dispatch)

Japanese Army in Shenyang Rushes to Haicheng

(Shenyang) At 8:30 p.m. last night, about 200 volunteer soldiers attacked the Haicheng concession. After fighting fiercely with the Japanese army for 30 minutes, they were repelled by the Japanese army. At 10:30 p.m., a large force of more than 1,000 men attacked again, surrounding and attacking the concession. The Haicheng police ordered 400 Japanese residents to take refuge in the ○○ team and urgently telegraphed the Kwantung Army headquarters for assistance. After receiving the telegram, the headquarters immediately ordered the Handa unit stationed in Shenyang and the "Manchukuo" Jing'an unit to rush to the aid from Shenyang at 12:00 a.m. last night. However, at 11:00 p.m. last night, the volunteer army surrounded the concession again from the east, west, and north. The South Manchurian Railway train to Dalian stopped at Anshan Station. Telegraphs and telephones were completely out of service, and communication with Haicheng was cut off. (3rd Electus News Agency dispatch)

Puppet State Aircraft Bombards Volunteer Army

The "Manchukuo" aviation team in Yingkou flew along the railway this morning for reconnaissance, discovering about 1,200 volunteer soldiers in squads of 200-300 hiding in sorghum fields. They immediately bombarded them from the air. The volunteer army suffered heavy losses. (3rd Electus News Agency dispatch)

Four Japanese Warships on High Alert

Yingkou The volunteer army, with the purpose of disturbing the South Manchurian Railway concession, surrounded the streets of Xinjing (unclear in the telegram, transliterated) and continued to stubbornly resist the joint attacks of the Yingkou garrison, marines, and Manchukuo army. The sound of artillery fire still rumbled this morning and did not stop. There was extreme anxiety in the city. Four Japanese destroyers are now on high alert for any eventuality. (3rd Electus News Agency dispatch)

Yingkou Artillery Fire Rages All Night

(Shenyang) On the morning of the 2nd, 1,500 volunteer soldiers attacked Yingkou. One Japanese police officer and three patrolmen were killed in action and were then repelled by the Japanese garrison and police force. At midnight, the volunteer army counterattacked from the south of Yingkou, attacking near the Japanese consulate. The Japanese garrison, marines, police force, and Manchukuo army cooperated to resist. At 1:00 a.m. on the 3rd, fighting was still ongoing, and the sound of artillery fire raged all night. The citizens felt extremely uneasy. The Manchukuo air force had dispatched from Shenyang at noon yesterday. Japan also dispatched destroyers from Huludao carrying marines to provide support. They landed at 2:00 p.m. on the 2nd and established a Marine Corps headquarters at the South Manchurian Railway office. (3rd Electus News Agency dispatch)

Chiang Arrives in Hankou by Ship Yesterday

Determined to Eradicate Red Bandits in Five Provinces Within Six Months

(Hankou) Chiang arrived in Hankou by ship on the 3rd and met with Cao Haosen, Xia Douyin, Wan Wu, the Director of the Henan Finance Department, and Guo Jijiao, the Chief of Staff of the 14th Army. It is reported that Chiang believes that the main force of the Red Bandits in central Hubei has been disintegrated and the elite troops have suffered losses. He is determined to eradicate the Red Bandits in the five provinces of Hunan, Hubei, Jiangxi, Henan, and Anhui within six months. (3rd Special Dispatch)

Zhang Liansan's Troops Defeat Duan Bandits

(Hankou) Military news, Zhang Liansan's troops defeated Duan Bandits in Huangjiaji, Jingmen. The remnants of the bandits fled to Pijiaji. Zhang Zhenhan's troops searched for Red Bandits and captured more than 100 members of the puppet government chairman and political workers in Luoshangwan, Taiheji. (3rd Special Dispatch)

Xianning and Minquan Warships Arrive in Hankou

(Hankou) The Xianning and Minquan warships arrived in Hankou on the 3rd. Gong Sheng sailed upstream. (3rd Special Dispatch)

Relief Funds to Aid Refugees in Bandit Areas

(Hankou) On the 3rd, He Chengjun telegraphed Xia Douyin, requesting that 100,000 yuan of flood relief funds be used to handle the recovery of bandit areas and to appease and relieve the people. He Hengfu, a member of the Flood Relief Association, has returned to Hankou to negotiate and will issue a notice through the association to persuade the flood victims stranded in Wuhan to return to their hometowns. (3rd Special Dispatch)

Promulgation of Measures to Appease Red Bandits

(Hankou) On the 3rd, the headquarters ordered the Pacification Headquarters to transmit to the various armies the measures for dealing with surrendering Red Bandits and the outline of the measures for those who were coerced and those who have reformed themselves, as resolved at the Lushan Conference, and ordered them to be implemented with reference to them. (3rd Special Dispatch)
